Context: The basis of life-the main component of protein is an amino acid molecule.It is an organic molecule.Although people have not directly observed amino acid molecules in cosmic space, scientists have used hydrogen, water, oxygen, methane and formaldehyde in the laboratory to simulate the natural conditions of space.Kinds of amino acids.The raw materials used to synthesize amino acids are abundant in interstellar molecules.It is not difficult to imagine that there must also be amino acid molecules in the universe.As long as there is an appropriate environment, they may be transformed into proteins and further develop into organic life.According to this speculation, there are living bodies on other planets than the earth, and may even be living bodies with higher intelligence.
Question: Which of the following is true to best refute the above speculation?
Choices:
  A: There is a huge difference between the process of developing from protein to organic life and the process from organic molecules to protein
  B: Higher intelligence is not only a product of material evolution, but also a product of continuous socialization
  C: In the natural environment, the synthesis of amino acid molecules from existing interstellar molecules is a small probability event
  D: Some interstellar molecules are not found in the Earth â€™s environment, and they are still not available in the laboratory

  Therefore, the answer is C: In the natural environment, the synthesis of amino acid molecules from existing interstellar molecules is a small probability event.

Context: Placebo effect" refers to the phenomenon of letting patients take fake drugs that have no effect at all without knowing it, but they can get the same or better effects than real drugs.The "placebo effect" has been supported by many clinical studies.One explanation for this phenomenon is that human expectations for the future will change the physiological state of the brain, which in turn will cause physiological changes throughout the body.
Question: The following statements can support the above explanation, except
Choices:
  A: The placebo effect is the result of a combination of factors.
  B: Placebo has no effect on Alzheimer's patients who have lost their expected future abilities.
  C: Some patients do not believe that the treatment will be effective.Although they have been treated normally, their condition has worsened.
  D: Inject the subject with normal saline and make him believe that it is an analgesic.The subject's brain then secretes the analgesic endorphin.
Response 0:

  D: This statement supports the explanation. The subject's belief that they are receiving an analgesic can change their physiological state and cause the brain to secrete endorphins.

Question: If the speeches of M and N are separated by lunch, which of the following lists all speakers that can be arranged between M and N?

  A: G, J
  C: F, G, J
  B: J, L
  D: F, G, J, L

  M and N are separated by only one speaker, so the other two speakers before lunch must be F and one of J or L, while the other two speakers after lunch must be the remaining two.
  Therefore, the only possible list of speakers between M and N is J and L.

  So, the only possible arrangement of speakers between M and N is G and J.
  The answer is A: G, J.

  A: Paper E is used, but paper H is not used.

Question: The following statements all weaken the conclusions above, except
Choices:
  A: Those women who often eat celery pay more attention to fitness, and fitness consumes a lot of physical energy, is very tired, and suppresses the aggressive mood.
  B: Female interviewees are susceptible to hints and are more willing to cooperate.They will cooperate with researchers intentionally or unintentionally to answer questions in the direction they want.
  C: Like the effect of placebo, eating celery will suppress the aggressive mood, which stimulated a series of psychological and mental activities of female respondents and made them feel less aggressive.
  D: Celery has the effects of calming the liver, clearing away heat, removing annoyance and reducing swelling, detoxifying the lungs, strengthening the stomach and blood, lowering blood pressure, and brain sedation.
Response 0:
Thought:
  The question asks for the statement that does not weaken the conclusions above.
  The conclusions of the study are that eating celery helps to suppress aggressive emotions and that women who often eat celery rarely have aggressive feelings or are irritated.

Context: In a cooking competition, the chef is required to make one hot dish and one cold dish, and the results are evaluated as "top grade", "middle grade", and "bottom grade".If each result of the chef is not lower than that of Chef B, and at least one item is higher than Chef B, it is said that "Chef A is more skilled than Chef B".There are a number of existing chefs, none of them is more skilled than the other, and no two people have the same hot dishes and cold dishes.
Question: How many chefs can meet the above conditions?
Choices:
  A: unconfirmed
  B: 9 people
  C: 6 people
  D: 3 people
Response 0:

  If there are n chefs, then there are n hot dishes and n cold dishes.
  No two people have the same hot dishes and cold dishes.
  Therefore, there are n! ways to assign hot and cold dishes to the n chefs.
  For each pair of chefs, there are 3 possible outcomes of their competition: Chef A is more skilled, Chef B is more skilled, or they have the same skill level.
  If no two people have the same hot dishes and cold dishes, then each pair of chefs will have a unique outcome.
  If each result of Chef A is not lower than that of Chef B, and at least one item is higher than Chef B, then Chef A is more skilled than Chef B.
  Therefore, for each pair of chefs, there is only one possible outcome where Chef A is more skilled than Chef B.
  If no two people have the same hot dishes and cold dishes, then there are n(n-1)/2 pairs of chefs, and each pair has a unique outcome.
  If no two people have the same skill level, then there are only 3 possible outcomes for each pair of chefs.
  Therefore, the maximum number of chefs that can meet the above conditions is the largest n such that n(n-1)/2 <= 3n.
  Solving for n, we get n <= 7.74.
  Therefore, the maximum number of chefs is 7.
  However, we need to check if there is a way to assign hot and cold dishes to 7 chefs such that no two people have the same skill level.
  This is a difficult combinatorial problem, and we cannot assume that such an assignment exists without further information.
  Therefore, the answer is A: unconfirmed.

Topic: Logic
Context: A unit arranges for 6 people on duty on the first day, second day, third day of the new year.They are G., H, K, L, P, and S.Two people are required per day.The personnel arrangement must meet the following conditions? (1) L and P must be on duty on the same day.(2) G and H cannot be on duty on the same day.(3) If K is on the first day of duty, then G is on the second day of duty.(4 ) If S is on the third day of duty, then H is on the second day of duty.
Question: If H is on duty the same day before S, which of the following must be true?
Choices:
  A: G on the second day of duty
  B: P on duty in the second day
  C: K on duty in the first day
  D: H on duty at the first day
Response 0:

  If S is on the third day of duty, then H is on the second day of duty. 
  Therefore, S must be on duty on the third day, and H must be on duty on the second day.
  The personnel arrangement must meet the condition that two people are required per day.
  Therefore, L and P must be on duty on the same day. 
  Since H is on duty on the second day, G cannot be on duty on the second day, because G and H cannot be on duty on the same day.
  If K is on the first day of duty, then G is on the second day of duty.
  Therefore, K cannot be on the first day of duty, because G cannot be on the second day of duty if H is on duty the same day before S.
  The only option left is P on duty in the second day.
  Therefore, the answer is B: P on duty in the second day.

Context: After all the cold dishes at the banquet at one table were served, there were 7 hot dishes.Among them, three Sichuan dishes? K, L, M? three Cantonese dishes? Q, N, P? one Shandong dish? X.Only one hot dish can be served at a time, and the order of serving must meet the following conditions? (1) Cannot serve Sichuan cuisine or Cantonese cuisine continuously.(2) Unless the second is on Q, P cannot be on before Q.(3) P must be on before X.(4) M must be on before K, and K must be on before N.
Question: If the third is M, which of the following statements may be true?
Choices:
  A: Fifth on X
  B: First on Q
  C: Sixth on L
  D: Fourth on K
Response 0:
Thought:
  If the third dish is M, then we can use the given conditions to determine the order of the dishes.
  Since M must be on before K and K must be on before N, we know that M must be the third dish, K must be the fourth dish, and N must be the fifth dish.
  Since we cannot serve Sichuan or Cantonese cuisine continuously, the first dish cannot be a Sichuan or Cantonese dish.
  Since P must be on before X, and M cannot be the first or second dish, we know that P must be the second dish, and X must be the sixth dish.
  Therefore, the only statement that may be true is C: Sixth on L.

  S P M K N C C X
  Now we have to serve a Cantonese dish. According to condition (2), P must be on before Q. So Q cannot be the next dish.
  The only option left is N. And then we can serve Q and L in any order.
  Therefore, the order of dishes is S P M K N C C X Q/L Q/L.
  Now, we can check which of the statements may be true.
  Statement A: Fifth on X - This is true.
  Statement B: First on Q - This is not true because we cannot serve Q before P.
  Statement C: Sixth on L - This is not true because we can serve L at the end, but not in the sixth position.
  Statement D: Fourth on K - This is not true because K comes after M and N.
  Therefore, the answer is A: Fifth on X.

Question: If the following items are true, all inconsistencies in the above may be reasonably explained, except
Choices:
  A: The private economy accounts for a large proportion of Zhejiang's economy, and the growth of some private economy is difficult to be counted.
  B: In order to leave room for economic development in the region, some local officials underreported the economic growth figures.
  C: Due to the sharp increase in energy prices, the economic growth of large state-owned enterprises with high energy consumption generally declined.?
  D: Due to the sharp increase in energy prices, 90% of the newly invested enterprises in Zhejiang are low-energy enterprises.
Response 0:
Thought:
  The article states that energy consumption and economic growth are positively correlated.
  The article also states that the difference in growth between energy consumption and economic growth is usually no more than 15%.
  However, in 2003, Zhejiang Province's energy consumption increased by 30%, while economic growth was only 12.7%.
  The question asks which of the following options cannot reasonably explain the inconsistency between energy consumption and economic growth.
  Option A suggests that some private economy growth is difficult to count, which could lead to inaccurate economic growth figures.
  Option B suggests that local officials underreported economic growth figures to leave room for economic development. This could lead to inaccurate economic growth figures.
  Option C suggests that high energy consumption state-owned enterprises may have experienced a decline in economic growth due to sharp increases in energy prices. This could lead to inaccurate economic growth figures.
  Option D suggests that 90% of newly invested enterprises in Zhejiang are low-energy enterprises. This could explain the discrepancy between energy consumption and economic growth.
  Therefore, the answer is D: Due to the sharp increase in energy prices, 90% of the newly invested enterprises in Zhejiang are low-energy enterprises. It can reasonably explain the inconsistency between energy consumption and economic growth.

### Temperature: 5.0 | Problem 75 of 100 ###
Topic: Logic
Context: A survey of traffic accidents has found that the incidence of traffic accidents is actually similar in cities where drunk driving is strictly investigated and those who do not.However, most experts believe that strict investigation of drunk driving can indeed reduce the occurrence of traffic accidents.
Question: Which of the following is most helpful in eliminating this inconsistency?
Choices:
  A: Severe investigations of drunk driving have occurred in urban traffic accidents.
  B: The city that implements strict investigation of drunk driving has not eliminated drunk driving.
  C: It is more important to improve drivers' traffic safety awareness than strict management.
  D: In addition to strict investigation of drunk driving, other traffic violations should also be stopped.
Response 0:
Thought:
  The survey found that incidence of traffic accidents is similar in cities with strict investigation of drunk driving and those without.
  However, experts believe that strict investigation of drunk driving can reduce traffic accidents.
  There seems to be an inconsistency between the survey results and the experts' beliefs.
  We need to find an option that can help resolve this inconsistency.
  Option A doesn't provide any new information that can help resolve the inconsistency.
  Option B suggests that even though strict investigation of drunk driving is implemented, drunk driving still exists, which doesn't help resolve the inconsistency.
  Option C is not relevant to the inconsistency between the survey and the experts' beliefs.
  Option D suggests that strict investigation of drunk driving alone may not be enough to reduce traffic accidents, and other traffic violations should also be stopped. This option provides a possible explanation for the inconsistency.
  Therefore, the answer is D: In addition to strict investigation of drunk driving, other traffic violations should also be stopped.
Action: Answer("D")

  The survey found that incidence of traffic accidents is similar in cities with and without strict investigation of drunk driving.
  However, experts believe that strict investigation of drunk driving can reduce traffic accidents.
  The inconsistency is that the survey result contradicts the experts' belief.
  To eliminate this inconsistency, we need to find an answer that reconciles the survey result and the experts' belief.
  Answer A does not help eliminate the inconsistency.
  Answer B may explain why the survey result is still valid despite the experts' belief. If a city has not eliminated drunk driving despite strict investigation, then that may explain why the incidence of traffic accidents is similar in cities with and without strict investigation of drunk driving.
  Answer C does not help eliminate the inconsistency.
  Answer D does not help eliminate the inconsistency.
  Therefore, the answer is B: The city that implements strict investigation of drunk driving has not eliminated drunk driving.

Topic: Logic
Context: There are 6 warehouses in a warehouse, in order from 1 to 6.There are 6 kinds of goods F, G, L, M, P, T.Each warehouse stores exactly one of 6 kinds of goods, and different kinds of goods cannot be stored in the same warehouse.The following conditions must also be met when storing goods? (1) The warehouse number for storing G is larger than the warehouse number for storing L.(2) The warehouse number storing L is larger than the warehouse number storing T.(3) The warehouse number storing P is larger than the warehouse number storing F.(4) The warehouse storing T is next to the warehouse storing P.
Question: If there is exactly one warehouse between the warehouse where M is stored and the warehouse where G is stored, how many kinds of goods are stored in the warehouse?
Choices:
  A: 2 rooms
  B: 3 rooms
  C: 4
  D: 5 rooms
Response 0:
Thought: 
  If there is exactly one warehouse between the warehouse where M is stored and the warehouse where G is stored, then there are only two possible arrangements for these two goods: M _ G or G _ M.
  From condition (1), we know that the warehouse number for storing G is larger than the warehouse number for storing L. Therefore, G cannot be stored in the warehouses 1, 2, or 3. This means that G must be stored in warehouses 4, 5, or 6.
  From condition (2), we know that the warehouse number storing L is larger than the warehouse number storing T. Therefore, L cannot be stored in the warehouses 5 or 6. This means that L must be stored in warehouses 1, 2, 3, or 4.
  From condition (3), we know that the warehouse number storing P is larger than the warehouse number storing F. Therefore, P cannot be stored in the warehouses 1 or 2. This means that P must be stored in warehouses 3, 4, 5, or 6.
  From condition (4), we know that the warehouse storing T is next to the warehouse storing P. Therefore, T and P must be stored in warehouses 3 and 4 in some order.
  Combining all the information, we can deduce that the only possible arrangement for the warehouses is F _ L _ T _ P _ G _ M.
  Therefore, there are 6 kinds of goods stored in the warehouse.

Question: If any of the following statements are true, can we best explain the above-mentioned violation of common sense?
Choices:
  A: On the evening of August 5, the US Treasury responded that S & P had a $ 2 trillion error in its rating calculations.
  B: Compared with the bonds of the European Union, Japan and other countries, US Treasuries are still relatively safe and liquid investment products.
  C: After the US sovereign credit rating was lowered, Russia began to reduce its holdings of US Treasury bonds, while China still increased its holdings of US Treasury bonds.

Topic: Logic
Context: Some people think that only by establishing a good institutional mechanism can corruption be fundamentally eliminated.However, once a trend is formed in Chinese society, even a powerful system will be torn apart by it."Correcting the people's hearts and then the world", in order to solve the problem fundamentally, "rectifying the people's hearts" must be taken as the foundation.Only when the hearts of the people are right can the winds of corruption and utilitarianism be eliminated, and the anti-corruption system can be truly established and effectively implemented.
Question: Which of the following statements is the assumption upon which the above argument relies?
Choices:
  A: There is corruption in any society, and no matter what method is used, it can only weaken corruption and not eradicate it.
  B: The formation of corruption and utilitarian winds is not caused by imperfect systems or imprecise implementation.
  C: The effective way to change the customs is to select the virtuous and competent, narrow the gap between the rich and the poor, and ideological education for profit.
  D: The system is fundamental to correct people's hearts.With the anti-corruption system and strict implementation, the atmosphere will change.
Response 0:
Thought: 
  The argument suggests that establishing a good institutional mechanism alone cannot fundamentally eliminate corruption.
  The argument suggests that correcting people's hearts is the foundation to solve the problem fundamentally.
  The argument suggests that only when the hearts of the people are right can the winds of corruption and utilitarianism be eliminated and the anti-corruption system can be truly established and effectively implemented.
  The assumption upon which the argument relies is that the formation of corruption and utilitarian winds is caused by imperfect hearts of the people and not by imperfect systems or imprecise implementation.
  Therefore, the answer is B: The formation of corruption and utilitarian winds is not caused by imperfect systems or imprecise implementation.

### Temperature: 5.0 | Problem 90 of 100 ###
Topic: Logic
Context: Homo erectus originated in Africa about 2 million years ago and spread to Eurasia; modern people appeared about 200,000 years ago.Both human fossils are distributed in China.For example, the "Beijing people" unearthed in the ancient stratum of Zhoukoudian, Beijing belonged to Homo erectus; the "shandingdong people" in the stratum of the previous year belonged to modern people.A study of the contemporary Chinese population found that the Y chromosome inherited from the paternal lineage originated in Africa and originated in 8.9 10,000 years to 35,000 years ago; the mitochondrial DNA inherited from the maternal line originated in Africa, with a time of origin within 100,000 years; no genetic component of H.erectus was detected
Question: If the above statement is true, which hypothesis is best supported?
Choices:
  A: The descendants of "Beijing people" may be extinct.The ancestors of Chinese contemporary people came to Asia from Africa about 100,000 years ago
  B: Chinese Homo erectus and modern people are from the African continent, and their hybrid descendants are the ancestors of contemporary Chinese
  C: The "Stop Cave Man" in Zhoukoudian, Beijing evolved from "Beijing People"
  D: Contemporary Chinese are descendants of Homo erectus that spread from Africa to Eurasia 2 million years ago
Response 0:
Thought:
  The statement mentions that Homo erectus originated in Africa and spread to Eurasia, and that modern humans appeared about 200,000 years ago.
  The statement also mentions that both Homo erectus and modern human fossils have been found in China, and that genetic studies of contemporary Chinese populations indicate an African origin for both paternal and maternal lineages.
  The statement explicitly states that "no genetic component of H. erectus was detected".
  Therefore, it is reasonable to conclude that contemporary Chinese are not descendants of Homo erectus, and that both Homo erectus and modern humans in China have African origins.
  The best-supported hypothesis is B: Chinese Homo erectus and modern people are from the African continent, and their hybrid descendants are the ancestors of contemporary Chinese.

  A: In the traditional cod fishing belt, a large number of seals caused great inconvenience to the fishing boat.
  B: The damage caused by seawater pollution to cod is more serious than that caused to seals.

  A: G
  B: J
  C: K
  D: L

Question: If the Finance Department is on the third level, which of the following may be correct?
Choices:
  A: The R & D department is on the fifth floor

  The Research and Development Department can be on either the fifth floor or above the Sales Department.
